<P STYLE="margin-top:24pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>COSTCO WHOLESALE CORPORATION REPORTS FIRST QUARTER </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:0pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman" ALIGN="center"><B>FISCAL YEAR 2020 OPERATING RESULTS </B></P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">ISSAQUAH, Wash., December&nbsp;12, 2019 - Costco Wholesale Corporation (&#147;Costco&#148; or the &#147;Company&#148;) (Nasdaq: COST) today announced its
operating results for the first quarter (twelve weeks) of fiscal 2020, ended November&nbsp;24, 2019. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net sales for the first quarter were
$36.24&nbsp;billion, an increase of 5.6&nbsp;percent from $34.31&nbsp;billion last year. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Comparable sales for the first quarter fiscal 2020 were as
follows: </P> <P STYLE="font-size:12pt;margin-top:0pt;margin-bottom:0pt">&nbsp;</P>

<TD ALIGN="left" VALIGN="top"> <P STYLE=" margin-top:0pt ; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman; " ALIGN="left">Excluding the impacts from changes in gasoline prices and foreign exchange. </P></TD></TR></TABLE>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Total and comparable sales were negatively impacted by approximately <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">one-half</FONT> percent due to Thanksgiving occurring a
week later this year. <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">E-commerce</FONT> sales in the quarter were negatively impacted by an estimated 12 percentage points. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Net income for the quarter was $844&nbsp;million, or $1.90 per diluted share, compared to $767&nbsp;million, or $1.73 per diluted share, last year. This
year&#146;s first quarter reflects a $77&nbsp;million ($0.17 per diluted share) tax benefit related to stock-based compensation, compared to a $59&nbsp;million ($0.13 per diluted share) similar benefit last year. </P>
<P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Costco currently operates 785 warehouses, including 546 in the United States and Puerto Rico, 100 in Canada, 39 in Mexico, 29 in the United Kingdom, 26 in
Japan, 16 in Korea, 13 in Taiwan, 11 in Australia, two in Spain, and one each in Iceland, France, and China. Costco also operates <FONT STYLE="white-space:nowrap">e-commerce</FONT> sites in the U.S., Canada, the United Kingdom, Mexico, Korea,
Taiwan, and Japan. </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">A conference call to discuss these results is scheduled for 2:00 p.m. (PT) today, December&nbsp;12, 2019, and is available via a
webcast on www.costco.com (click on Investor Relations and &#147;Play Webcast&#148;). </P> <P STYLE="margin-top:12pt; margin-bottom:0pt; font-size:10pt; font-family:Times New Roman">Certain statements contained in this document constitute
forward-looking statements within the meaning of the Private Securities Litigation Reform Act of 1995. For these purposes, forward-looking statements are statements that address activities, events, conditions or developments that the Company expects
or anticipates may occur in the future. In some cases forward-looking statements can be identified because they contain words such as &#147;anticipate,&#148; &#147;believe,&#148; &#147;continue,&#148; &#147;could,&#148; &#147;estimate,&#148;
&#147;expect,&#148; &#147;intend,&#148; &#147;likely,&#148; &#147;may,&#148; &#147;might,&#148; &#147;plan,&#148; &#147;potential,&#148; &#147;predict,&#148; &#147;project,&#148; &#147;seek,&#148; &#147;should,&#148; &#147;target,&#148;

indicated by such statements. These risks </P>
